## OPENING & THE MORNING LETTER

The investigators have the [manuscript](#the-locked-study) and the knowledge that [Don Eusebio](REF-NPCs.md#don-eusebio-valdez) must stand in the closing ritual's outer ring. They met **[Héctor](REF-NPCs.md#h%C3%A9ctor-r%C3%ADos) and [Marta](REF-NPCs.md#marta-r%C3%ADos)** at the fence line last night ([Ch 4](#the-wrong-returned--first-appearance)). They slept at the estancia. **This chapter opens the next morning**, then follows them east toward the [Jesuit mission ruins](#the-jesuit-mission-ruins). Héctor and Marta travel with them. [Silvio](REF-NPCs.md#silvio-m%C3%A9ndez) stays at the estancia, watching the south pasture until he can't hold back — then walks south, toward the pit, not the ruins. Keep track of where Silvio goes.

### A letter from Buenos Aires _(run before they ride out — not optional)_

[Tomás](REF-NPCs.md#tom%C3%A1s-arredondo) finds the investigators at first light with a letter that arrived yesterday; he sat on it because Don Eusebio was shaken and Tomás didn't know what to do with mail in the middle of a confrontation.

It is from **[Doña Mercedes Solís](REF-NPCs.md#do%C3%B1a-mercedes-sol%C3%ADs)**, Universidad de Buenos Aires, addressed to _"El Sr. Don Eusebio Valdez, Estancia La Esperanza."_ Dated three weeks ago.

> _"Estimado Sr. Valdez: Aldao Quirce me ha enviado parte de la correspondencia que él mantiene con usted, sin su consentimiento. Le adjunto copia. Me llamó la atención una nota al margen de la página 47 del manuscrito de Saens — Quirce la transcribió. Si la lectura de Quirce es correcta, esa palabra cambia mucho. Hay una segunda voz dispuesta a ayudar — no la suya. Si necesita una segunda opinión sobre lo que está sucediendo en sus tierras, puede escribirme a la dirección abajo. — M.S."_
> 
> _"Dear Sr. Valdez: Aldao Quirce has sent me part of the correspondence he is maintaining with you, without his knowledge. I am enclosing a copy. A marginal note on page 47 of Saens's manuscript — which Quirce transcribed — caught my attention. If Quirce's reading is correct, that word changes a great deal. There is a second voice willing to help — not his. If you need a second opinion on what is happening on your lands, you may write to me at the address below. — M.S."_

_(The "word" Mercedes alludes to but does not write is **Necronomicón**. She writes around it on principle; she will name it only in person or in a sealed reply. Players who found the [marginal note in C4](#the-locked-study) recognize what she means; others will be drawn back to page 47.)_

Don Eusebio has not replied. He hands the letter to the players: _"Si pasa algo y yo no estoy, escríbanle ustedes. Ella es de fiar. Quirce no."_ Mercedes is the campaign's eventual moral and intellectual center; this introduces her as a name early. Players who write to her receive her **reply** later this chapter ([Mercedes' reply](#doña-mercedes-reply)).

> † _Canon note: in the published version, a parallel thread has Kuyen preparing ritual components and warning that the entity is "pushing — every night harder." That information (the entity is escalating; the pit is needed now) reaches this table instead through [the warning without Kuyen](#the-warning-without-kuyen) at chapter's end._

---

## THE WRONG RETURNED

### Morning after (or first approach)

If the party **already spoke with Héctor and Marta at the fence** ([C4 night beat](#the-wrong-returned--first-appearance)), open with them falling in alongside the horses as the party leaves — no re-introduction. Use the dialogue below for questions not yet asked, or for sustained daylight conversation on the road. If the party **has not yet approached them**, they spent the night standing at the fence without sleeping; in the morning they are still there:

> 
> _Se dan vuelta para mirarte antes de que los llames. Al mismo tiempo. No sobresaltados — sabían que venías. De cerca, son exactamente como los describió Rosa: comen, contestan preguntas, se quedan parados al sol sin molestia aparente. Pero hay algo en el foco de su atención que está mal de una manera que cuesta un momento nombrar. Te están mirando a vos, y también mirando algo que ocupa el mismo espacio que vos pero que no sos del todo — una geometría de tu posición en el espacio, más que tu cara._

**Appearance**:

- **Héctor Ríos**, 54. Former farmer from San Ruiz, wide-shouldered, graying. Was considered steady — not smart but reliable. Now answers questions with precise answers and no small talk; he has lost the social texture around his speech — the _"pos"_, the pauses. He just answers.
- **Marta Ríos** (his wife, no relation — the surname coincidence was a village joke), 43. Was the village teacher and midwife. Calm by profession; calmer now in a way that is not professional. The more present of the two — occasionally something that was Marta crosses her face and is gone.

**What they know**: not everything. They know what the entity showed them — geometrically accurate but not experientially interpretable. They speak in architecture and space, not sensation.

Héctor: _"No está bajo tierra. Eso estaba mal. Está en los ángulos. Vive en los lugares donde una superficie se encuentra con otra. El pozo es solo donde la forma es más grande — donde hay suficiente ángulo para que pase por ahí."_

Marta: _"Hay otros como nosotros. No muchos. Los que tocó pero no se llevó. Seguimos acá. Pero también estamos en parte allá."_

Héctor: _"Volvimos porque ya casi es la hora. Lo sentimos desde Tres Lagunas. El cierre, o la apertura. Una de las dos va a pasar. Tenemos que estar en la geometría cuando pase."_

**What they want**: to be at the pit for the final event — closing or opening, no preference. They are not aligned with the entity; they are anchored to the geometry. Their presence at the closing will matter ([Ch 9](#chapter-9--el-cierre)).

**The question no one wants to ask** — what happens to them when the geometry is sealed? Marta, without distress: _"No sé. Si la forma se cierra, capaz nos cerramos con ella. Capaz volvemos. Decidimos que no importa. Tenemos que estar ahí."_

**SAN Check**: 0/1D3 (sustained conversation with someone who is and isn't a person).

**Possible Q&A**

_"Do you remember what happened to you?"_

> Héctor: _"I remember walking south. The night was very clear. And then it was like — like someone showed me a map of a place I'd been trying to describe without words. It was a relief, for a moment. And then I was back and it was morning."_ Marta: _"I remember it differently. There was no relief in mine. Only size. Something very large noticing something very small."_

_"Are you in pain?"_

> Héctor: _"No."_ _(Too quickly, too finally.)_ — _"No."_ _(Dicho demasiado rápido y demasiado terminante.)_ Marta: _(A long pause.)_ _"I don't feel pain the way I used to. I'm not sure if that's better."_ — _(Una pausa larga.)_ _"No siento dolor como antes. No estoy segura de que eso sea mejor."_

_"Can you be helped?"_

> Marta: _"You could close the geometry. Maybe that ends this. Or maybe this is what we are now and closing it just removes the sound."_ _(She touches her own face as if checking it's still there.)_ _"Close it anyway."_ _(Se toca la propia cara como comprobando que sigue ahí.)_ _"Ciérrenla igual."_

---

## EL POMBERO ON THE RIDGE

On departure, after Héctor and Marta have fallen in. The road east skirts a low rise — a _cuchilla_ the locals call _El Pelón_, "the bald spot," because no grass grows on its crown. Tomás doesn't look at it as you ride past; Don Eusebio's _peones_ won't speak its name. As the horses round its base, a small figure appears at the top — not climbing, simply _there_:

> 
> _Es bajo. Piel morena, cara ancha, un sombrero de paja demasiado grande para su cabeza. Levanta una mano y saluda — ni amistoso, ni amenazante, solo reconociendo que están pasando. Silba. El silbido tiene más notas de las que una persona debería conocer._

**[El Pombero](REF-NPCs.md#el-pombero)** is the guide-and-test. He does not _do_ anything yet — he whistles, waves, vanishes when looked away from. **Spot Hidden** while passing: the grass on _El Pelón_'s crown has the same ring pattern as the cattle field's rings — older, smaller, the same shape. _El Pelón_ is a _previous_ burial pit, ten generations old. **Do not open an entrance here.**

Tomás, if pressed, strangled: _"El Pombero. Le silba a los que están por entrar a algo. No me pregunten más."_

> **Roll for Hound** ([table](#roll-for-hound--c5)): if a Marked PC looks hard at the ring pattern, or the party camps in sight of the rise — both Marked PCs roll 2d6.

---

## THE ROAD TO THE RUINS

The Jesuit mission ruins are a day's ride east and slightly south; Saens's notes give landmarks (a forked river, a mesa that looks like a tooth) still accurate. The Wrong Returned walk alongside, requiring no water stops, keeping pace without effort.

> 
> _La tierra entre la estancia y las ruinas es pampa común — pasto chato y seco, algún matorral bajo de vez en cuando. Pero si viajás con Héctor y Marta, empezás a verla a través de su atención. Registran las esquinas. No de manera dramática — una mirada cuando el camino dobla, un instante de quietud donde una meseta proyecta una sombra en ángulo recto. Leen la geometría de la tierra como un hombre de campo lee el pasto buscando humedad._

**Optional encounter — the road**: during the night camp, a [Luz Mala](REF-NPCs.md#la-luz-mala) appears to the south — not orbiting, stationary, ~200 m distant. Watching. It followed from the estancia. Héctor, without fear: _"Es un sensor. No es una amenaza salvo que toques la geometría."_ It tracks them all the way to the ruins.

### The merchant with tarnished copper (5b)

Late in the day's ride — the tooth-shaped mesa visible, the ruins an hour ahead — the party meets **Don Crisanto Larrea** before the stones.

> 
> _Un carro chico está apartado del camino al abrigo de una cuchilla baja, el eje apoyado en una piedra. Un hombre canoso de unos cincuenta y pico está revisando su mercadería con la cara de quien ya perdió una discusión con el día. Levanta la vista cuando se acercan. No busca un arma. Busca el sombrero._

**Backstory (if asked)**: a traveling merchant on the Tandil–Buenos Aires road — _yerba_, copper _bombillas_, buttons, kettle-fittings, a few iron tools. His axle cracked two days east. He limped to the [ruins](#the-jesuit-mission-ruins), spent **last night** camped inside the broken walls, and was leaving this morning when the copper went wrong.

> 
> _Cada objeto de cobre se ennegreció durante la noche — no el verde del óxido natural, negro, parejo, como si lo hubieran tenido a la llama una hora. Las bombillas quedaron inservibles, los botones opacos, los herrajes arruinados. Las herramientas de hierro, intactas. La yerba, bien. **Solo el cobre, y solo el cobre que estaba del lado del carro que daba al piso de la capilla** — la piedra tallada junto a la cual durmió sin saber qué era. El cobre del otro lado está normal._

Larrea is bewildered — twenty years a merchant, never seen this: _"Dormí al lado de esa piedra en el piso. No la toqué. Esta mañana el cobre del lado de la piedra estaba así. Es como si algo hubiera mirado el cobre toda la noche. ¿Saben? Como si el cobre hubiera estado mirándolo a él también."_

**Héctor or Marta** (if present): a glance at the chapel, then the copper — _"The stone is still doing work. So is the copper now."_ No more unless pressed.

> **What this is**: the [dual diagram](assets/dual-diagram.svg) under the chapel floor _recognized_ the copper as metallically similar to [Quirce's](REF-NPCs.md#aldao-quirce) brass markers and tried to extend through it overnight. A **Hard Cthulhu Mythos** roll identifies the same geometric-extension effect as Quirce's markers — but here, without markers, pulled from _below_. Marked PCs may feel it unprompted.
> 
> **What investigators can do**: buy the ruined copper at scrap price (Larrea is grateful). Brought to the [bone chamber](#the-bone-chamber) later, it _re-tarnishes_ on contact with the walls — confirming the link. [Mercedes](REF-NPCs.md#do%C3%B1a-mercedes-sol%C3%ADs) will later recognize the signature.
> 
> **Larrea's onward role**: he limps east toward Buenos Aires once trade is done, arriving in the city before the players do, two months later. He tells the tarnished-copper story to the _vigilantes urbanos_ at the gate; it reaches [Saráchaga](REF-NPCs.md#don-eladio-sar%C3%A1chaga), who writes Mercedes that _"the pressure is now visible at the perimeter, not just at the centre."_ This is one of the threads that brings Mercedes to the camp in [C7](#doña-mercedes-arrives-late). Larrea is the campaign's first non-Keeper, non-curandera, non-tribal civilian witness to the entity's reach. He never knows what he saw. He dies of natural causes in 1843.

**Placement**: run on the **approach** (end of road) or as the **first beat at the ruins** — whichever fits pacing.

---

## THE JESUIT MISSION RUINS

> 
> _La misión fue abandonada en 1767, cuando los jesuitas fueron expulsados. Lo que queda: las piedras de cimiento de cuatro edificios, un campanario roto que todavía se sostiene en parte, paredes que llegan a la altura del pecho y nada más. La piedra es caliza pálida, distinta de la roca de la zona — la trajeron hasta acá. Quien construyó esto eligió este lugar a propósito._
> 
> _La vegetación dentro de las ruinas es distinta — más densa, más verde a pesar de la estación. Acá crecen cosas que no deberían crecer tan al sur — una higuera, improbablemente, en el rincón de lo que fue la capilla. Como si la tierra acá fuera más **fértil**._
> 
> _Esa palabra. Otra vez esa palabra._

**Keeper notes**:

- The standing bell tower is the most intact structure. The bell itself fell and lies half-buried in the grass, inscribed **1749** — twelve years before the mission was built. It was brought from elsewhere.
- The chapel foundation has carved stones worked into the floor — flush with the others but different: the limestone has the geometry carved into it. These are the originals Saens found. The mission was built _on_ them.

### The carving

> 
> _Cuando encontrás la piedra tallada — y la vas a encontrar, porque Héctor camina derecho hacia ella — es a la vez más chica y más precisa de lo que esperabas. Unos sesenta centímetros de ancho, hundida en el piso de la capilla. El tallado es profundo y limpio: la misma geometría angular y circular, pero acá está completa. Tanto el diagrama de apertura como el contra-diagrama, al mismo tiempo — uno dentro del otro, interactuando. Como una cerradura y una llave talladas en la misma piedra._
> 
> _Es, sin lugar a dudas, la cosa más precisa que viste hecha a mano en tu vida._

> **Visual handout**: [dual-diagram.svg](assets/dual-diagram.svg). Print large (A4 min, A3 if possible). This is the carved stone; what Marta finger-traces at midnight; what they will see in bone in the [bone chamber](#the-bone-chamber); what Buenos Aires _becomes_ in [C12](#chapter-12--el-libro). Show it — do not describe it.
> 
> **Roll for Hound**: Marked PC looks hard at the stone, or page 79 read **aloud** — both Marked PCs roll 2d6.

**Skill checks**:

|Skill|Result|
|---|---|
|Occult|Not two competing symbols — one symbol. The opening and closing are two aspects of the same geometry, like a door and a doorframe. The opening is not wrong. It is **incomplete**.|
|Cthulhu Mythos|The geometry predates human habitation of the region by a very long time. Who carved it — before Saens, before the Tehuelche — has no answer in any tradition this character knows.|
|History|The limestone does not exist within 200 km. It was brought from the north. The stone was carved _elsewhere_ and installed here.|
|Art/Craft (Drawing)|The precision is geometric in the mathematical sense — the angles are _exact_. The tools of any human period should not produce this quality of line.|

**Héctor**, hands on the stone (the only one who touches it without hesitation): _"Acá es donde vive la forma. El pozo es solo donde alguien le abrió un agujero."_

**Marta**, from across the room: _"Padre Saens tenía razón en una cosa. No es el diablo. Pero se equivocó en otra. Dijo que era una herida. No lo es. Es una puerta. La herida es lo que le hicimos nosotros."_

---

## DEEP READ: THE MANUSCRIPT

> **Saens notes**: [player handout](02-la-salamanca/padre-saens-manuscript-player.md) · [keeper](02-la-salamanca/padre-saens-notes-keeper.md)

Cross-referencing the manuscript with the carved stone makes additional passages legible:

**Page 71 (margin — illegible until the carved stone is in sight)**:


**Page 72 (water-damaged — now partly reconstructable)**:


This is the chapter's key revelation: the Wrong Returned are **structural components of the closing ritual**. Their presence at the outer ring stabilizes the geometry against the entity's pressure in a way trained humans cannot replicate. This changes their status from victims-to-be-protected to agents-with-a-role.

**Page 79 (final legible line)**:


**SAN Check** (reading this line): 0/1 — recognition of what Saens felt, and what it means that the investigators are the "next one."

### Reader-path seed (Use ending, C12)

The PC who reads **page 79 aloud at the table**, in the GM's hearing, has — without anyone explaining it, including the GM — taken the first step into the **Reader role** available in C12 (Use ending). The PC does not know this; the Marked PCs do not see it; **[Mercedes](REF-NPCs.md#do%C3%B1a-mercedes-sol%C3%ADs) recognizes it later** ([C8](#chapter-8--la-traición)). From this point, when the reader looks at _any_ ritual text (Saens's manuscript, Quirce's notebook, Mercedes's parchment, the Necronomicón's binding section in C12), the words **stay in their head verbatim, in Saens's voice**. This is the campaign's quietest seed and pays off in C12.

> **Disambiguation**: if multiple PCs read page 79 aloud, the seed lands on the one who reads _slowest_, with the most weight, in the most silence — willingness to bear, not skill. **If no PC reads it aloud** (here or over the skull below), the Reader path is **closed** in C12: only Hide and Destroyed are available. This is the only campaign branch C5 choices can close. **Make a Keeper note about whether the seed was planted. Do not retrofit.**

_(Second and final chance to plant the seed is the [reading-over-the-skull](#reader-path-failsafe--reading-over-the-skull) failsafe in the bone chamber.)_

---

## THE NIGHT AT THE RUINS

_(optional)_

If investigators camp at the ruins, the night brings a single event. At ~2 AM, Marta wakes and walks toward the chapel ruin. She doesn't go inside; she stands at the threshold and traces the air with her finger — the complete dual diagram, from memory, in the dark, in three dimensions, eyes open but focused on something not there.

When she finishes, not to anyone, in the way [La Llorona](REF-NPCs.md#la-llorona) spoke: _"Catorce personas fueron al campo de noche. Siete volvieron cambiadas. Cinco de esas no sobrevivieron al cambio. Dos sí. Yo soy una de las dos."_ She returns to her bedroll and appears to sleep.

**SAN Check**: 0/1 — not frightening, just unbearably sad.

> **Roll for Hound**: Marta tracing the geometry in air — both Marked PCs roll 2d6.

---

## DESCENT AT THE CARVED STONE

After the deep-read (and the night, if run). The players understand the dual diagram; Héctor or Marta shows them what it does.

> 
> _Marta camina hasta el piso de la capilla al mediodía — el único momento en que el anillo exterior del diagrama doble no atrapa ninguna sombra. Se arrodilla junto a la piedra. Apoya las manos en dos puntos específicos — los dos donde los arcos de apertura y de cierre se cruzan. Aprieta. La piedra no se mueve. La tierra alrededor de la piedra se mueve._
> 
> _Un cuadrado de tierra y pasto, de dos metros de lado, se hunde unos quince centímetros. Después gira — el cuadrado entero, alrededor de la piedra, noventa grados — y debajo aparece un pozo vertical. Revestido en piedra. Más viejo que la capilla. Cae hacia la oscuridad. El aire que sube huele al mismo filo mineral que la fosa, y a otra cosa que no se huele desde hace siglos: incienso frío, hecho de una resina que no crece en este clima._

**Héctor, if asked**: _"Esto es lo que llaman La Salamanca. No es una sola — hay varias. Esta es una de las antiguas. Una de las que se hicieron antes de que los Jesuitas hicieran su capilla encima."_

**Observable (before descent)**: a half-full canteen placed on the carved circle shows its water forming _standing waves_ in the dual-diagram pattern — the fluid reading the geometry the way iron filings read a magnet. The waves persist as long as the canteen sits there. No roll. Show the SVG beside it.

This is the **entrance to La Salamanca**. The shaft drops to the [bone chamber](#the-bone-chamber).

> **Roll for Hound**: when the square **rotates** and the shaft opens — both Marked PCs roll 2d6 immediately.

---

## EL POMBERO RETURNS

As the players prepare to descend, El Pombero is sitting on a ruin wall, whittling a stick — not seen since [El Pelón](#el-pombero-on-the-ridge). Without looking up:

> _"Abajo se baja con preguntas, no con armas. Si llevan armas, igual bajen. Pero no van a servir."_

If asked what is below: _"Lo viejo. Lo que estuvo antes de los curas, antes de los charrúas, antes de los tehuelches. La gente que vino primero. No queda nadie de ellos. Pero la geometría queda."_

Three warnings — all useful, none specific:

1. **[The bone chamber](#the-bone-chamber)** holds the dead of the previous closing attempt. Do not disturb the bone alignment; they are still doing work.
2. **[The whispering tunnels](#the-whispering-tunnels)** beyond it are not haunted, but they _amplify_ — every whisper is heard by all, in their own voices. Speak carefully.
3. **[The Great Wizard's chamber](#the-chamber-of-the-great-wizard)** at the deepest point has been closed for decades. Do not seek it this chapter. _"No están listos. Yo tampoco."_

Then, looking up for the first time: _"Abajo aprenden. Arriba deciden. Después **vuelven al oeste** — al agujero que ya abrieron. No se queden acá admirando la piedra."_

He vanishes between two glances. Marta: _"He has been here longer than the carving. Don't ask how."_

---

## THE BONE CHAMBER

The shaft drops twelve meters to a roughly six-meter hexagonal chamber, walls of the same imported limestone as the Saens stone above, ceiling low enough that players bend slightly. The floor is **bones, in the dual diagram's pattern**.

> 
> _Los huesos están dispuestos formando el diagrama doble completo, a escala del piso. Hay quizá doscientos — huesos largos, cráneos, vértebras, entremezclados deliberadamente a mano. Los cráneos están en las posiciones del anillo exterior. Miran hacia adentro. No son humanos — demasiado largos, demasiado angostos en la mandíbula, las cuencas demasiado separadas. No son de ninguna especie que los jugadores puedan nombrar._
> 
> _En el centro mismo del diagrama, donde alguien debe arrodillarse como ancla en el cierre, hay un único cráneo humano. Viejo. Humano moderno. La frente sin marcas. **Es el Padre Ignacio Saens.** Volvió acá, solo, el año antes de morir, y se acostó sobre el diagrama en lugar de la gente que no tenía — el que abre, el que sostiene el conocimiento y la contra-figura, todo a la vez — y compró el tiempo que pudo. Su cuerpo fue tomado por la geometría como sustituto. El cráneo es la única parte que quedó porque la geometría necesita un centro, y el hueso de un hombre aguanta donde el pergamino no._

**SAN Check**: 1/1D6 — for what Saens did, alone, ahead of the players, knowing it would not be enough.

> **Observable**: lanterns brighten ~30% at the chamber center (over Saens's skull) and dim ~30% at the outer ring. No draft. Lit cigars draw smoke _inward_ toward the central skull rather than rising — the geometry is breathing.
> 
> **Geometry points west** _(run this — do not wait to be asked)_: any compass brought underground **drifts west** — the bearing of [Estancia La Esperanza](REF-NPCs.md#don-eusebio-valdez) and the burial pit. Not broken; _pulled_. Marked PCs feel it as a tug in the chest. **This is the campaign telling them where the closing happens.** The teacher is here; the wound is west.
> 
> **Larrea's copper**: if bought, it _re-tarnishes_ on contact with the chamber walls — confirming the link to the pit geometry.

### Explaining the diagram — Marta and Héctor

**When to run**: after the first long look at the floor. Run **proactively** if players are quiet or treating this as a museum; also if anyone asks what the bones mean, where the closing happens, or who stands where. Héctor and Marta do not lecture unprompted, but they will answer, and they read the floor the way a midwife reads a room.

**Handouts** (lay beside Saens's skull):

|Print|Use when explaining|
|---|---|
|[`dual-diagram.svg`](assets/dual-diagram.svg)|Full shape — "this is what you're standing on"|
|[`dual-diagram-opening.svg`](assets/dual-diagram-opening.svg)|Triangle up, three pressure points|
|[`dual-diagram-closing.svg`](assets/dual-diagram-closing.svg)|Outer ring, triangle down, eastern weak arc|
|[`dual-diagram-anchor.svg`](assets/dual-diagram-anchor.svg)|**Center** — place on or beside the human skull|

Héctor kneels at the edge of the pattern, not on it. He does not touch the skull. He points with two fingers, not touching:

> _"Arriba en la capilla viste el dibujo en la piedra. Acá es el mismo dibujo, en hueso. Misma forma. Tres cosas en una."_

If you spread the split handouts, he taps each in order:

1. **Opening** — _"La apertura. Lo que sale. No es el diablo saliendo — es el espacio abriéndose para que algo pase. El cura lo llamaba herida. No es herida. Es puerta."_
2. **Closing** — _"El cierre. El anillo. Estos cráneos miran adentro porque el cierre mira adentro. Cuando cierren en el pozo, necesitan esto alrededor — gente en el anillo, no solo palabras."_
3. **Anchor** (place on Saens's skull) — _"La ancla. El centro. Donde alguien se queda quieto y sostiene todo el dibujo en un solo lugar del mundo. Sin centro, la forma flota. No cierra."_ He looks at the human skull; his voice does not change, but the room tightens. _"El Padre Saens se acostó acá porque no tenía a nadie más. Compró años. No cerró."_

**Marta**, if still confused, crouching beside Héctor (still not on the pattern):

> _"Piensen en el pozo de la estancia. Ustedes abrieron la puerta ahí. El dibujo de arriba enseña la forma. El pozo es donde la forma tiene que **quedarse** cuando la cierren. El centro del pozo es esto."_ _(She taps the anchor handout on Saens's skull.)_ _"Alguien arrodillado. Alguien que no se mueva."_

**The center, named plainly** — Héctor:

> _"En el arroyo había un muchacho que se arrodillaba en el centro. Ya no está. Alguien más tiene que hacer eso en el pozo — el que abrió el agujero, o uno de ustedes."_

Marta, quieter:

> _"[Don Eusebio](REF-NPCs.md#don-eusebio-valdez) tiene que estar en el anillo de afuera de todos modos. El centro puede ser él. O puede ser quien aguante mirar hacia adentro sin correr. Yo puedo sostener un costado del anillo. Héctor el otro. No somos el centro. Somos lo que evita que se mueva."_

This is the campaign's **role map** for C8–9 in one conversation: Eusebio outer ring (minimum); center = Eusebio or volunteer PC; Héctor/Marta = outer anchors (necessary, not sacrificial).

> † _Canon note: the center anchor at the published creek-bed closing was Nahuel, who is dead at this table; the mechanic (the closing needs a still center or the shape "floats" and won't seal) is unchanged — it now falls to Don Eusebio or a volunteer PC._

**If players ask specific questions**

|Question|Who|Line|
|---|---|---|
|_"Is this where we close it?"_|Marta|_"No. Acá aprendieron. El cierre es en el pozo — al oeste. La brújula lo sabe."_ / _"No. You learned here. The closing is at the pit — west. The compass knows."_|
|_"Can we move Saens's skull?"_|Héctor|_"No."_ _(Beat.)_ _"Sigue trabajando."_ / _"It is still working."_|
|_"What are the three pressure points?"_|Marta|_"Arriba, en la piedra. Donde yo apreté para abrir el pozo. Apertura. No los uses acá."_ / _"Upstairs, in the stone. Where I pressed to open the shaft. Opening. Do not use them here."_|
|_"Why the eastern arc marked on the closing diagram?"_|Héctor|_"El este cede primero. En el pozo también. Cuando vuelvan, miren el este antes que nada."_ / _"The east gives first. At the pit too. When you go back, look at the east before anything else."_|
|_"Do you two stand in the center?"_|Marta|_"No. Nosotros somos anclas del borde. El centro es más pesado. Alguien con más… o más culpa."_ / _"No. We are edge anchors. The center is heavier. Someone with more… or more guilt."_|

**SAN**: no extra check for the lesson (the 1/1D6 above covers Saens). If a PC **kneels on the center** imitating the anchor: **0/1** — recognition, not horror.

**Keeper context — what Saens achieved**: the closing requires three roles (opener, knowledge-holder, counter-figure); Saens stood in for all three. What he produced was a **partial binding** that held ~6 decades, sustained afterward by [Antu-Rayo](REF-NPCs.md#antu-rayo)'s lineage. Don Eusebio's ritual eight months ago widened a wound already opening. The bone chamber is not a finished closing — it is the cost of a brave, incomplete one. A **Hard Cthulhu Mythos** roll on the non-human skulls: they are _"the first people"_ — the species that carved the original geometry, before any human reached the Pampas. Each transmission of the tradition lost detail; the full closing was never available to humans alone. This is the strongest argument that **the Necronomicón may hold the full ritual** — and the most likely place it survives is Buenos Aires.

### The Bone Vigil (_De Vigilia Ossium_) — hidden rite

**Discovery**: a limestone niche the size of two fists in the **south wall**, easy to miss. **Spot Hidden (Regular)** or **Search (Hard)** after the diagram lesson, or when anyone searches the walls.

> _Inside: a roll of waxed cloth, stiff with age. Unrolled: three sheets in Saens's hand — a draft, not part of the bound manuscript. The ink is greener than the study folios. The title: **De Vigilia Ossium**. Figura I shows the closing ring walked clockwise; Figura II shows a kneeler beside a skull, not on it. A Mapudungun phrase is boxed: **Antu kishu, lan amukey**. At the bottom, in a shaking hand: Scripsi hoc postquam solus iacui. Alius vigilabit. — "I wrote this after I lay down alone. Another will keep vigil."_

**Handout**: [`bone-vigil-rite.svg`](assets/bone-vigil-rite.svg).

**What it is**: a **closing-aspect** rite — counterpart to the opening-aspect [Graveyard Kiss](01-la-tierra-mala/diagrams.md#the-graveyard-kiss-de-osculo-sepulcrali--eusebios-locked-study-page) in Eusebio's study. Saens drafted it after his first solo attempt failed, before he lay down to die. It closes nothing. It lets the geometry **answer one honest question** about the scar at La Esperanza.

**Héctor**, if read aloud: _"El cura lo escribió para quien viniera después. No para él."_ He will not stop them.

**Requirements**: a complete dual diagram underfoot (the bone floor qualifies; a traced pit copy does not unless drawn at Hard Occult) · a **kneeler** beside Saens's skull (never on it, never moving it — Héctor intervenes if they try) · a **walker** with a long bone from the floor, touching each outer-ring skull once, **clockwise**, starting at the eastern station · kneeler speaks **Antu kishu, lan amukey** (Antu-Rayo's fragment — the line [Mercedes](REF-NPCs.md#do%C3%B1a-mercedes-sol%C3%ADs) leads at the pit in C8) and holds **thirteen breaths** without moving · then **one honest question** about the La Esperanza scar, spoken aloud.

|Step|Detail|
|---|---|
|**Roll**|**CON (Hard)** for the kneeler; the walker needs no roll unless they disturb a skull|
|**Cost**|Kneeler: **1D6 SAN, 1D4 HP** (geometry presses inward) · Walker: **0/1 SAN**|
|**On success**|The chamber answers **once**, truthfully — not in speech: pressure, image, compass-pull, or a sentence in the kneeler's own voice from the wrong direction. Give a **true** short answer (east fails first, Eusebio must stand in the outer ring, Quirce's asymmetry, what the pit wants)|
|**On failure**|Kneeler cannot rest that night; **both Marked PCs roll 2d6** for Hound|

**Benefits**: if a [Tier-1](#if-they-disturb-the-bones) disturbance was triggered, then restored, then the vigil completed in the same scene → **no eastern penalty** from that disturbance. A kneeler who succeeded may treat **one** eastern-segment CON check at the pit ([C8](#chapter-8--la-traición)) as **Regular** instead of Hard (once per campaign). **Cost**: like the Graveyard Kiss, each performance teaches **El Patrón** the performer's hand. Low-level, not free.

> _Do not push this rite. Let them find the niche. Make the answer worth the SAN — and make clear it is **one question**, not a hotline._

### If they disturb the bones

Expect this. The default outcome is **not** a full Hound manifestation — it is a short, survivable **cataloguing pass** ([entity ref](assets/entity-hound.md)). The entity is not hunting; it is checking what changed in a diagram it already knows.

**Before they touch anything** (run if a hand reaches toward the floor):

> **Marta** _(flat)_: _"No los muevan. Siguen trabajando."_ **Héctor**: _"El Pombero lo dijo. No es respeto — es mecánica."_

|Tier|What they did|Immediate effect|Entity?|
|---|---|---|---|
|**1**|One outer-ring bone shifted, kicked, replaced wrong|Lanterns **dim 50%** at that station; cold along that wall; the bone **vibrates** once|Optional 2d6|
|**2**|Several moved, opening triangle broken, long bones scattered|**Cataloguing pass** (1 round) automatic; partial binding **weakens**|Automatic|
|**3**|Saens's skull moved, taken, or sat on|**Cataloguing pass** (2 rounds); Héctor may **physically intervene** (STR opposed — he won't hurt them, but won't let the skull leave); binding **weakens badly** if skull leaves|Automatic + both Marked PCs roll 2d6|

**Grave sin** (pocketing multiple bones, smashing a first-people skull "for proof"): Tier 3 + **SAN 1/1D4** + cataloguing pass runs **3 rounds**; the disturber gets a **catalogue-mark** — their shadow falls 15° wrong in any active geometry until the pit closes. Survivable. Memorable.

**The cataloguing pass** _(survivable — not combat)_. Use **instead of** a full Hound. The entity has been _notified_ the diagram changed; it comes to **read the edit**, not to feed.


**Duration**: 1 round (Tier 1 on failed 2d6), 2 rounds (Tier 2–3), 3 rounds (grave sin).

**What players can do each round** (pick one): **Hold still** (no roll, safest — it finishes reading and leaves) · **Freeze on an intact bone** (stand on an undisturbed outer-ring position — automatic; it already has them on file) · **Replace what you moved** (DEX or Art/Craft Regular — one bone back per success, each ends the pass one round early; Marta coaches for +1 bonus die) · **Throw fire toward the angle** (no roll — entity retracts from that surface 1 round; does not end the pass) · **Run** (CON Regular — running manufactures angles; on fail, 0/1 SAN and the pass extends 1 round) · **Attack** (weapons pass through — wasted round) · **Marked PC "looks hard"** at it (do not, unless you want escalation — raised 2d6 threshold + POW roll or 0/1D3 SAN, lose next action).

**When it ends**: cold lifts; lanterns return to normal breathing. Disturbed bones **left in the chamber** _creep_ — not animate, _settle_ — toward their original positions over 10–30 minutes (audible scrape; unsettling, not lethal). Bones **carried out** do not return. **SAN**: 0/1 per PC (Tier 1–2), 1/1D3 (Tier 3 / grave sin) — not gore, _being read_. **Marked PC private read**: _It was not angry. It was updating. You were not the subject. The gap was._

**Carry-forward — weakened binding** (the price at the pit — friction, not death):

|Tier|Effect at the C8/C9 closing|
|---|---|
|**1** (repaired before leaving)|No penalty if bones restored before exit; otherwise eastern segment **one step harder** for one phase|
|**2**|Eastern segment **one step harder** for the whole working. Mercedes (C7+): _"Someone taught the scar an interruption. The east will remember."_|
|**3** (skull moved but returned)|As Tier 2, plus center-anchor CON check **one step harder** for whoever kneels|
|**3** (skull **removed** from chamber)|As above, plus **no partial-binding backup** at the pit — the closing must stand entirely on its own|

**Repair before leaving** (reduces tier one step, min Tier 1 → no penalty): **Marta** replaces the pattern from memory — 1 hour, silence, no tunnel exploration meanwhile. She does not ask permission; she starts when they stop arguing. _"Sé dónde iban. Mi cuerpo lo sabe."_ / _"I know where they went. My body knows."_ (Cannot fix Tier 3 if the skull is gone — bring it back first.)

**Héctor after Tier 2+** (if they survive the pass): _"No fue un castigo. Fue un inventario. Ahora el dibujo tiene un borrador en el margen — y el pozo lo va a leer cuando lleguen."_

> **Log the bone-disturbance tier (0–3).** It carries to C8 as east-friction.

### Reader-path failsafe — reading over the skull

> Run this **only if no PC read page 79 aloud at the ruins**. If the seed was already planted, skip. This is the second and final chance before the path closes permanently.

After the diagram lesson settles and the party has looked at Saens's skull a while, Marta looks at whoever holds the manuscript — not asking:

> _"Él escribió para el que viniera después. Nadie se lo leyó nunca en voz alta. Léanselo. Acá. Él está acá."_

She means **page 79** ([handout H2](assets/handouts-c5-c7.md#h2--manuscript-page-79-the-readers-page)), read aloud, over the skull, in the chamber's silence. If a PC reads it — slowly, with weight — the **Reader-path seed is planted** exactly as the ruins version would have. Note the PC's name; log it. If multiple read, the seed lands on the slowest, heaviest reading. If the table declines both invitations (ruins + skull), the path is closed honestly — they were asked twice. **Do not retrofit.**

> **Roll for Hound**: reading page 79 aloud _inside the bone chamber_ — both Marked PCs roll 2d6. The geometry is already awake; the skull is a resonator. **Double 1** → cataloguing pass (1 round) on the last syllable. It is not angry. It heard.

---

## THE WHISPERING TUNNELS

The passage beyond the bone chamber runs deeper — ~2 m tall, smooth-walled, ceiling carved with the dual diagram's outer ring repeated at one-meter intervals. It is _acoustically tuned_: every word spoken in the tunnels is repeated at the mouth of each chamber ahead, in the speaker's voice, at the original volume.

Practical effect: any roll involving speaking in the tunnels is **one step harder** — the speaker hears their own words returned in real time. **A Listen roll** identifies the tuning; silence works as a navigational tool.

Beyond the bone chamber the way **does not fork** — it is a single descending spine. Each room opens off the last; the only forward passage from each lies past that room's feature. They pass through everything, in order, or they do not go on.

**1 · Offering chamber.** Stone table with a cup, bone needle, clay tablet in unreadable script. **Hard Library Use** identifies **proto-Tehuelche**, but the script is older than known proto-Tehuelche by perhaps a thousand years. Permanent campaign object — Mercedes will want to see it. *(Keeper: the cup + bone needle are the **toll-prep kit** for the guardian two rooms on. A party that lingers here is rewarded later.)*

**2 · Whisper tunnel — vizcachas & a voice.** The acoustic tuning has teeth here: the warren in the walls comes for noise.

| Party behaviour | Result |
|---|---|
| Quiet / using Stealth | No swarm. No roll. |
| Loud / not using Stealth | **Hard group Luck.** Fail → swarm. |

> **Swarm (low-level, survivable):** **1 pt/round** engulfed; the real cost is the **light** — Luck or DEX each round to keep a lamp lit (losing it is the penalty). **SAN 0/1.** Break free by going still or reaching the next room — **they do not leave the tunnels.** **No Hound roll.** (Retroactively explains Tomás's stone coming from a *vizcachera* in C1.)

In this tunnel the party meets the **[antiquarian PC](pc-antiquarian-entry.md)** — a voice returns at the tunnel mouth that none of them spoke, a man reading Latin under his breath. He came in by a **second cave mouth** on his own research; the **back path collapsed behind him**, so the party's route is now his only way out (the collapse can be why the warren is stirred up). He hands them the vizcacha rule in-fiction and warns of what waits:

> *"Hablen bajo — los túneles están llenos de vizcachas y vienen por el ruido. Y hay algo encadenado en la oscuridad pasando el próximo hueco. No se me vino encima. Sólo esperó. Tráiganle algo, o no creo que los deje pasar."*

> **Keeper:** keep his Latin **muttered**, not aloud-at-the-table — protects the Reader-path seed being planted this chapter. Make it an incantation only if you want him in the running as a future Reader.

**3 · The guardian — El Invunche.** See **[The Guardian — El Invunche](#the-guardian--el-invunche)** below. The toll is the encounter; the offering chamber was the answer.

**4 · Flooded chamber.** Floor dropped; groundwater chest-high. Submerged: another dual diagram, same scale as the chapel stone — intact and *still active*. A witness-stone (Arc 4) lowered here would read warm. *Observable*: pampas grass dropped on the water will not sink; it arranges into a small dual-diagram on the surface within thirty seconds. **This is the descent's Hound room** — entering the active flooded diagram triggers the roll (both Marked PCs, 2d6).

**5 · The antechamber & the sealed door.** The spine ends at a low chamber where the whispering **stops** — silence is worse. The **[sealed door / Great Wizard's chamber](#the-chamber-of-the-great-wizard)** is set in the far wall. This is as far ahead as the antiquarian got: he has been standing at the slab unable to make his hand open it. The door remains the one real **choice** of the descent — default, leave it sealed and move on.

**Marked PC in the tunnels**: speaking quietly, they hear their own words returned — with a _second_ voice underneath, faint, in the rhythm of the outer ring (twelve syllables, pause, twelve syllables). They will recognize this rhythm at the closing ([C8](#chapter-8--la-traición)) and at the dock ([C12](#chapter-12--el-libro)).

> **Roll for Hound**: first spoken word in the tunnels under stress; Marked PC notices the twelve-syllable undertone; entering the flooded chamber with the active diagram — both Marked PCs roll 2d6.

---

## THE GUARDIAN — EL INVUNCHE

*Low-level encounter. The toll is the encounter, the claws are the punishment for skipping it. Stat block: [npc-stats.md — El Invunche](assets/npc-stats.md#el-invunche--guardián-de-la-salamanca).*

> *Algo está plegado en la oscuridad del fondo, donde sigue el pasaje. Se despliega — mal. La cabeza doblada del todo hacia atrás, mirándote por su propia columna. Una sola pierna; el otro miembro cosido o crecido al costado. Hace un sonido que no es palabra, porque la boca de donde sale no tiene lengua. No se abalanza. Se planta en el único camino adelante y espera, con paciencia de animal, lo que le vas a dar.*
>

**SAN 0/1D4** to see it. **The gut-punch (separate, +0/1D4):** the moment a PC registers it was **made, not born** — milk-teeth, a child's garment-scrap. Let it land in silence; let the players do the math. A **Psychology** read: it does not guard out of malice. It was *placed.* Being fed is the only kindness it has known.

**The toll — what it accepts, and what it costs:**

| Offering | Works? | Cost |
|---|---|---|
| **Bone needle + cup** *(offering chamber)* | ✅ Intended | A pricked finger: **1 HP** + a beat of dignity. No curse, no fight. |
| **Fresh meat / charqui / bled finger** | ✅ Always | A ration, or **1 HP** if PC blood. |
| **Milk** *(folkloric Invunche food)* | ✅ Best | Placates *and calms* it — no curse risk on a fumbled exit. (Goat is at La Esperanza; milk must be carried in.) |
| **A page from a book** | ✅ | It presses the page to the tongueless mouth and keeps it. You've **fed a page to a guardian** — bites later if needed. **Do not let page 79 go without consequence.** |
| **A true name spoken aloud** | ✅ | In a whisper tunnel a name **carries** — risk it reaches the seal or wakes the warren. Marked PC's own name: Keeper's-option unease, log it. |
| **Empty hand / refusal / force** | ❌ | **The curse** (below) + the grapple→bite cycle. |

> **The curse (handout wording):** Refuse the toll or force past, and the Invunche lays its *maldición*. **Opposed POW 65 vs the target's POW×5.** On its success: **penalty die to ALL rolls until they leave La Salamanca**, and **−1D10 Luck**. It can cast this on a screaming, fighting party as its action — this, not the 1D6 claw, is how a careless fight actually hurts.

**Three ways through (all viable):**
1. **Pay the toll** *(intended)* — tribute from the offering chamber. No fight. The antiquarian flagged it.
2. **Fight it** — slow, no Dodge, weak-ghoul HP; the curse + grip make a loud brawl costly. **Killing it ends the toll permanently — and the Wizard will know his guardian is dead** (he greets the door differently in C6).
3. **Slip past silent** — Stealth vs its **Listen 75%**. Hard: the whisper tunnel broadcasts every sound. Same silence law as the vizcachas.

> **[THIS TABLE]** The Invunche **confirms the brujería layer before the door** without spending the Wizard reveal — it cannot speak. Do **not** let it carry Coypac / eastern-asymmetry intel; that stays behind the slab. No Hound roll in this room.

---

## THE CHAMBER OF THE GREAT WIZARD

_(optional — run only if investigators force the sealed door after [Pombero's warning](#el-pombero-returns))_

> **Warn at the table**: this is the deepest human layer of La Salamanca; what they learn here cannot be unlearned; [C6](#quirce-arrives) will feel different if they have already met the Wizard or read his desk.

### Keeper brief — who he is

_Full NPC: [REF-NPCs](REF-NPCs.md#the-great-wizard-of-salamanca) · stats: [npc-stats.md](assets/npc-stats.md)._ Mortal head of the **Cult of the Great Sleeper** (the players don't know that name yet). A scholar-priest in late old age who built a school in La Salamanca's deepest chamber and believes he is recovering pre-colonial knowledge that will _re-found_ the _campaña_ outside the Spanish-Catholic frame. He is sincere, learned, and **not insane** — the campaign's proof that intelligence is not protection. Ash-blond hair (same cast as the Coypac priests); robes of undyed wool with **ochre** edging (his signature); fingertips black with ink and ash; moves slowly (DEX 35). He wants a successful _observation_ at the estancia closing — not to stop it, but to ride its geometry while the Coypac awakening lights up in parallel. He does **not** know he serves [El Patrón](REF-NPCs.md#el-patr%C3%B3n--don-eligio-dad%C3%A1lah), who has steered him for forty years; every "discovery" was placed for him.

**Relationships**: correspondent and unwitting courier _via_ Quirce (the Wizard rides his ink, El Patrón rides his voice — they do not coordinate); unknown rival of Mercedes (whose youthful 1781 copy is the ultimate source of his fragments — she confesses this in [C11](#chapter-11--la-decisión)); known to El Pombero, who serves an older tradition El Patrón exploited.

### The door

The antechamber ends in a **slab of imported limestone**, flush with the wall, no handle. The dual diagram is carved into it, but the opening and closing arcs are **reversed** from the surface stone: a _seal_, not an entrance marker.

|Approach|Result|
|---|---|
|Brute force|Fails. The slab is not heavy — it is _anchored_. The geometry holds it.|
|Occult / Cthulhu Mythos|Recognizes a deliberate counter-seal; someone with full knowledge could open it from outside at the two intersection points, as Marta opened the shaft.|
|Marta or Héctor|Either can open it without a roll by pressing the two intersection points — then hesitating. Marta: _"This door was closed for a reason. The reason is still in there."_ If the party insists, they comply.|
|Wrong gesture (opening ritual traced on the seal)|The slab sinks and rotates like the surface entrance — but only 30 cm. A Hard POW roll or 1 MP: the opener feels the seal _recognize_ them as not the owner. Opens fully on a second attempt or with Marta/Héctor's help.|
|Marked PC|Feels the seal as a second skin over something that has been breathing on the other side for decades. **SAN 0/1** if they open it anyway.|

When it opens, the whispering **stops** in this tunnel. Silence is worse.

### The chamber

> 
> _La sala es más grande que la cámara de huesos — octogonal, el techo alto para pararse derecho. No es una tumba. Es un estudio. Estanterías talladas en la caliza sostienen códices, fascículos, mapas de la pampa con marcas en Estancia La Esperanza, San Ruiz, y un tercer sitio al este en la cordillera rotulado con una letra que no reconocés: **Coypac**. Un escritorio de tierra apisonada revestido en piedra. Lámparas sin combustible usadas hace poco — las mechas tibias. Sobre el escritorio: correspondencia en dos manos. Una es la cifra de Aldao Quirce. La otra es más vieja, más prolija._
> 
> _El aire huele a incienso frío y hierro. El piso no es de huesos. Es **ocre** — un diagrama doble completo en pigmento mineral, más fresco que todo lo de arriba. En el arco este, una línea está trazada **mal** a propósito: una corrección que solo haría alguien que conoce el dibujo desde adentro._

**Skill checks on the desk** (same content as the [C6 notebook scene](#quirces-move) — if found here, don't repeat verbatim at the estancia):

|Skill|Result|
|---|---|
|Library Use / Cthulhu Mythos|Three margin notes in the **Wizard's hand** on copied Saens pages: (1) _"This is from the third chapter of Alhazred. A copy survives. I have seen it."_ (2) _"The closing as Saens has it is incomplete. The full closing requires the page across from this one in Alhazred."_ (3) _"If Quirce can be persuaded to leave the geometry alone for one closing, I can make a successful observation. The book is then closer than it has ever been."_|
|History|The maps are current — within the last year. Someone has been walking the land.|
|Spot Hidden|A folded undyed-wool robe on a peg behind the door, ochre at the hem. A travel pack ready to leave.|

**SAN Check**: 0/1 — the ochre floor is _active_; lantern light bends toward the eastern correction.

**Is he here?** Roll **1D100** (or choose): **01–35 present** (at the desk, reading; he looked up when the seal moved — not surprised, only tired); **36–100 absent** (warm lamps, open ink; the seal reports to its maker, so he will know someone entered).

**If present**, he does not attack. He gestures to the stone seats — an old teacher's habit:

> _"El Pombero les dijo que no estaban listos. Tiene razón. Pero ya están acá, así que voy a tratarlos como estudiantes, no como ladrones."_

He answers direct questions with unsettling honesty. He does **not** name El Patrón; he does not know he serves him.

- _"Who are you?"_ → _"Soy el que lleva cuarenta años leyendo lo que Saens no pudo cerrar. Me llaman el Mago de la Salamanca."_
- _"What are you doing?"_ → _"Aprendiendo. Saens abrió una herida con la mitad de un libro. Yo busco la mitad que falta. No para abrirla más — para entender qué se puede cerrar y qué no."_ _(He believes this.)_
- _"The Necronomicón."_ → _"He leído partes. No tengo el libro. Tengo copias — algunas buenas, algunas corruptas. Una cadena de manos que no controlé. Si llegan a Buenos Aires, pregúntenle a alguien que haya leído el original. No a Quirce."_
- _"Coypac?"_ → _"Un sitio viejo. Más viejo que los Jesuitas. Allí se puede observar lo que acá solo se puede tocar. No les digo más — si van antes de tiempo, arruinan la observación."_
- _About the eastern line_ → _"Saens cerró sin el este. Siempre falla por el este primero. Lo corregí en mis copias. Quirce las llevó al pozo sin saber que llevaba mi mano."_ _(This is the eastern-asymmetry intel, delivered early.)_

**SAN Check** (sustained conversation): 0/1D3 — not horror of form, but horror of _competence in the wrong direction_.

**If threatened — combat in the chamber.** He reaches for the geometry, not a weapon, and will **not** duel to the death here; his goal is **time to open the crawl-space** behind the desk and vanish.

> **Great Wizard** — STR 35 · CON 45 · SIZ 55 · DEX 35 · INT 95 · POW 120 · EDU 100 · HP 10 · MP 24 · Move 4 · Dodge 25% · Occult 90% · Mythos 70%. **Chamber geometry (always on)**: his geometry spells one step easier; attacks/spells against him while he stands on the ochre one step harder; he regains 1D3 MP per round in contact with the ochre. **Escalation**: warning → illusion → suggestion → deflection → Mindblast → flee. By round 3 he is through the crawl-space; the ochre smears where he stood (still active). If reduced to HP ≤ 5 or out of MP, he opens a partial seal and squeezes out, gone.

**If a player casts Shrivelling** — the ochre **recognizes** hostile magic the way it recognized Larrea's copper. **Deflection of the Ochre** (his prepared counter, once per scene, automatic if the caster stands on the ochre):

> 
> After a successful deflection, calm: _"Eso no es cómo se habla con un maestro. Pregunten, o váyanse."_ He will not cast Shrivelling first; if attacked again he may cast it once in desperation (6 MP, CON resist, 1D8+) then flee regardless. Other spells: **Veil of Not-Quite** (opposed POW — target acts against empty air 1 round) · **Mental Suggestion** (opposed POW — one command, cannot attack) · **Mindblast** (2D6 SAN; lose next action if SAN loss ≥ 5) · **Dread** (CON — flee 1D3 rounds).

> **Roll for Hound — key geometries** (each Marked PC rolls 2d6; double 1 → 1D3-round peripheral cataloguing pass at the ochre-wall angle or crawl-space mouth, SAN 1/1D4; **not** a full C3 manifestation): Shrivelling cast on the ochre · the seal forced · the crawl-space opened · the eastern correction touched/traced (d2 if a Marked PC looked hard at it) · fight spilling back up into the bone chamber.

**If absent — what they still get**: the desk correspondence, maps, ochre floor, and eastern correction are enough. Leave a **Listen** beat as they leave — someone breathing in the crawl-space behind the desk, then silence.

**Consequences of opening (carry forward)**:

- **Quirce (C6)** arrives knowing someone breached Salamanca — his notebook annotations may be stripped or defensive.
- **Mercedes**, if written to, replies with urgency: _"You were not meant to find that room yet. Destroy nothing. Copy what you can. Do not trust what he told you about the closing."_
- **Eastern asymmetry**: a rubbing of the ochre floor is proof, and earns [Rosa](REF-NPCs.md#rosa)'s trust faster on the [second San Ruiz pass](#san-ruiz--second-pass).
- **El Patrón** may take interest (optional: a Luz Mala follows them out; a Marked PC dreams of a man in a Salta merchant's coat watching from the ridge).

> **C6 overlap**: if this scene ran in full, **shorten** the C6 [notebook](#quirces-move) and [eastern-asymmetry](#the-eastern-asymmetry-recognized) beats — the information is already in play. Keep the [mediumship](#the-mediumship); the players now have context for the second voice on Quirce's strings.

---

## THE ASCENT READING

_(scheduled — Session 5's guaranteed encounter)_

Run **as the party exits the shaft at dusk** — skip it only if the cataloguing pass or the Wizard fight already ran. It closes the gap where the second half of the session could otherwise end without a single encounter.

> _The party climbs out carrying knowledge the chamber did not have loose in the world an hour ago — and the geometry registers the withdrawal. As the last PC's head clears the shaft, the light over the ruins goes wrong: the shadows of the chest-high walls fall **at angles the sun does not justify**. For **1D3 rounds**, [El Sabueso](assets/entity-hound.md) executes a cataloguing pass on the surface — peripheral, at the angle where the chapel wall meets its own shadow. It reads each PC in turn (for the Marked: the sensation of being read _page by page_). It does not attack unless attacked. Fire or breaking line-of-sight ends it early._

**SAN**: 1/1D4 each. **Marked PC private read**: _It is not stopping you from leaving. It is noting what leaves._ **Roll for Hound**: none — this _is_ the manifestation; do not stack a 2d6 on top.

> **Carry-forward**: the Hound has now read the party **with the diagram lesson in their heads**. In C8 it goes to the east _first_ — it knows they know.

---

## DOÑA MERCEDES' REPLY

While the players are at the ruins, a runner from the post road delivers a letter forwarded from the estancia — from **[Mercedes](REF-NPCs.md#do%C3%B1a-mercedes-sol%C3%ADs)**, replying to whoever wrote to her after the [first letter](#opening--the-morning-letter). (If no one wrote, she writes anyway, alerted by Quirce's correspondence.) Two pages; key passages:

- _"La red de Quirce no es lo que él dice. Documenta 'anomalías geométricas' con fines sobre los que la red no se ha puesto de acuerdo. Algunos quieren cerrarlas. Otros quieren estudiarlas y aceptar el costo. Quirce pertenece a la segunda categoría. Considérenlo honesto en cuanto a sus observaciones y mentiroso en cuanto a sus intenciones."_
- _"Lo que Saens llamaba la figura está en el Necronomicón. He leído partes. No puedo decir dónde se encuentra ahora. Sí puedo decir que el ritual de cierre que parecen preparando servirá para **esta** apertura, pero no atenderá la cuestión más amplia. Hay más de una cicatriz. El libro las describe todas. El libro no es seguro y no se puede destruir con los medios a nuestro alcance. Lo guardamos; no lo usamos; lo mantenemos donde no pueda ser movido."_
- _"Si llegaran a estar en Buenos Aires una vez terminado esto, escríbanme. Los recibiré. Hasta entonces: cuídense de Quirce, y escuchen al Pombero — es, a pesar de las apariencias, la parte más honesta de su situación."_
- _"No acampen en las ruinas admirando el diagrama. Ya vieron al maestro. La herida que abrieron está en La Esperanza — vuelvan al oeste, prepárense ahí, y no dejen que Quirce decida el calendario por ustedes."_

**Runner from the estancia** (same delivery, or a second note): [Tomás](REF-NPCs.md#tom%C3%A1s-arredondo) sends a boy on a tired horse. The south pasture was **silent** again last night — no cattle sound at all. Grass rings wider than a week ago. A sealed letter from [Quirce](#quirces-announcement-letter) is on the sala mantel (_"within five days"_). Tomás's note, block hand: _"Vuelvan. El patron no duerme. Quirce viene."_

**SAN Check**: 0/1 — the casualness of _"I have read parts of the Necronomicón."_ Hand out the letter and Tomás's note:

> **HANDOUT H1 — Mercedes' first reply**
>
> *"La red de Quirce no es lo que él dice que es. Documenta 'anomalías geométricas' con fines sobre los que la red no se ha puesto de acuerdo internamente. Algunos de sus miembros quieren cerrarlas. Otros quieren estudiarlas y aceptar el costo. Quirce pertenece a la segunda categoría. Considérenlo honesto en cuanto a sus observaciones y mentiroso en cuanto a sus intenciones.*
>
> *Lo que Saens llamaba la figura está en el Necronomicón. He leído partes del Necronomicón. No puedo decir dónde se encuentra ahora. Sí puedo decir que el ritual de cierre que parecen estar preparando servirá para esta apertura, pero no atenderá la cuestión más amplia. Hay más de una cicatriz. El libro las describe todas. El libro no es seguro y no se puede destruir con los medios a nuestro alcance. Lo guardamos; no lo usamos; lo mantenemos donde no pueda ser movido.*
>
> *Si llegaran a estar en Buenos Aires una vez terminado esto, escríbanme. Los recibiré. Hablaremos de lo que viene después. Hasta entonces: cuídense de Quirce, y escuchen al Pombero — es, a pesar de las apariencias, la parte más honesta de su situación.*
>
> *No acampen en las ruinas admirando el diagrama. Ya vieron al maestro. La herida que abrieron está en La Esperanza — vuelvan al oeste, prepárense ahí, y no dejen que Quirce decida el calendario por ustedes.*
>
> *— M.S."*
>

> **HANDOUT H3 — Tomás's note**
>
> **"VUELVAN. EL PATRON NO DUERME. QUIRCE VIENE."**
>
> *"COME BACK. THE PATRON ISN'T SLEEPING. QUIRCE IS COMING."*

## THE WARNING, WITHOUT KUYEN

This scene puts two things in the players' hands before the closing: **(1)** return west — the pit at La Esperanza, not the ruins, is where the work happens; **(2)** the eastern segment of the binding is the weak side, and it is already failing. Run **all three deliveries (A + B + C)** in order as the party surfaces, then [the departure](#departure--return-west).

> † _Canon note: at the published table the curandera Kuyen delivers both points in person at the camp; she is dead at this table, so the same information arrives off the world itself, through the three deliveries below._

**Delivery A — the goat.** The [goat](REF-NPCs.md#la-cabra-the-goat) that has followed the party since [San Ruiz](#chapter-2--las-señales--la-capilla) has been watching the geometry all along. As the investigators emerge with the dual-diagram knowledge, she stands at the ruins entrance and will not move. A Marked PC who looks sees the six pupils (three per eye) tracing the carved stone's shape — and lingering on its **eastern arc**, returning to it, returning to it. She holds still ~thirty seconds, fixed on the east, then turns and continues following. The Marked PC understands they were just shown which side gives first.

> **SAN Check** (Marked PC watching the pupils track): 0/1 — recognition, not terror.

**Delivery B — Saens's late note.** Among Saens's papers in the [bone chamber](#the-bone-chamber), a Spot Hidden or careful re-read surfaces a final marginal entry not reached before — a sketch of the pit at La Esperanza with the eastern segment circled twice, and beneath it:

> _"El nudo del este siempre cede primero. La tradición de los Custodios lo llama el lado de la apertura — el que permite que algo entre, y el que necesita refuerzo antes del cierre. Sin ayuda en el este, el símbolo no cierra."_ **SAN Check** (reading it aloud): 0/1.

**Delivery C — La Llorona as signal.** [La Llorona](REF-NPCs.md#la-llorona), displaced from San Ruiz and moving east toward the pit, passes near the ruins. She cannot speak; she is not an ally and not a threat in this moment. But a Marked PC feels her passing as a **directional pull — east, toward the pit** — and in that pull the geometry of the creek bed and the burial pit lights up briefly, the eastern arc flickering like a flame that won't catch. A map, and a warning about which line is thin.

> **SAN Check** (Marked PC feeling the pull): 0/1.

**After A + B + C**, name the takeaway explicitly at the table: _return to La Esperanza, days not weeks, east is the side that fails, Quirce is inbound._ No living teacher hands it to them — they read it off the world — but say it out loud in the departure beat so nobody leaves fuzzy.

### Departure — return west

> 
> _Héctor ya dio vuelta el caballo hacia el oeste. Marta está a su lado. No están esperando permiso. "Ya tienen lo que vinieron a buscar. La forma bajo la capilla es la misma forma del pozo — sintieron la brújula. Este lugar enseña. La estancia sangra. No vamos a acampar acá otra noche. Ustedes tampoco deberían."_

If investigators argue for staying (more exploration, the wizard chamber, "we need to understand more"):

- Marta: _"Understanding without closing is how Saens died alone on the floor below us."_
- Héctor: _"The pit is pulling harder than this stone. I can feel it from here. So can you, if you stop pretending you can't."_ (Marked PCs: **automatic** — the westward tug intensifies as he speaks.)
- The [goat](REF-NPCs.md#la-cabra-the-goat), if present, has already walked west and stopped on the road — looking back once, then continuing.
- The [Luz Mala](REF-NPCs.md#la-luz-mala) on the southern horizon **does not follow them east** into open pampa; it stays between them and the ruins entrance — a sensor, not a chase. The message is spatial: _nothing more to learn here right now._

**If they still won't leave** (escalate): a westward cattle-sound hallucination at night (SAN 0/1); a Marked PC's dream in which the dual diagram unfolds and maps onto La Esperanza from above — the chapel stone a thumbnail, the pit the tear (SAN 0/1); at dawn, Marta opens the shaft to **close** it from inside (reverse of the descent) — _"The teacher gave the lesson. The door stays shut until you're ready at the wound."_ They can reopen it later; the point is narrative force.

**They must leave knowing**: the closing happens at the **estancia pit**, not the ruins (compass west · page 71 · Pombero · Héctor's departure); **return west** is the next move; **days, not weeks** (Saens's eastern note · the runner, grass rings widening); **east fails first** (deliveries A/B/C); **Quirce is inbound** (the runner + [his letter](#quirces-announcement-letter)); and the Wrong Returned **go west with or without them**.

---
